Look at the `loadMailDetails` function in MailIndexer.ts at lines 714-758.\n\nThe issue is in lines 733-739 (mailDetailsBlobs) and lines 749-755 (mailDetailsDrafts):\n\nFor mailDetailsBlobs:\n```typescript\nconst mailDetailsBlobs = await this.loadInChunks(MailDetailsBlobTypeRef, listId, ids)\nresult.push(\n\t...mailDetailsBlobs.map((mailDetailsBlob) => {\n\t\tconst mail = assertNotNull(mailDetailsBlobMails.find((m) => isSameId(m.mailDetails, mailDetailsBlob._id)))\n\t\treturn MailWrapper.details(mail, mailDetailsBlob.details)\n\t}),\n)\n```\n\nAnd `loadInChunks` (lines 780-791):\n```typescript\nprivate loadInChunks<T extends SomeEntity>(typeRef: TypeRef<T>, listId: Id | null, ids: Id[]): Promise<T[]> {\n\tconst byChunk = splitInChunks(ENTITY_INDEXER_CHUNK, ids)\n\treturn promiseMap(\n\t\tbyChunk,\n\t\t(chunk) => {\n\t\t\treturn chunk.length > 0 ? this._entity.loadMultiple(typeRef, listId, chunk) : Promise.resolve([])\n\t\t},\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tconcurrency: 2,\n\t\t},\n\t).then((entityResults) => entityResults.flat())\n}\n```\n\nThe problem is that when calling `this._entity.loadMultiple()`, no `providedOwnerEncSessionKeys` map is being passed! The mail's `_ownerEncSessionKey` is available (it comes from the parent Mail entity), but it's not being forwarded to the loadMultiple call.\n\nCompare with the correct approach in `src/mail/model/MailUtils.ts` at lines 404-411:\n\n\n```typescript\n} else {\n\tconst mailDetailsId = neverNull(mail.mailDetails)\n\n\tconst providedOwnerEncSessionKeys = new Map<Id, Uint8Array>()\n\tprovidedOwnerEncSessionKeys.set(elementIdPart(mailDetailsId), assertNotNull(mail._ownerEncSessionKey))\n\treturn entityClient\n\t\t.loadMultiple(MailDetailsBlobTypeRef, listIdPart(mailDetailsId), [elementIdPart(mailDetailsId)], providedOwnerEncSessionKeys)\n\t\t.then((d) => MailWrapper.details(mail, d[0].details))\n}\n```\n\nThe MailUtils approach correctly creates a map with the session key and passes it to loadMultiple. The indexer needs to do the same—build a providedOwnerEncSessionKeys map from the parent mail entities and pass it along when loading the details blobs.\n\nI should write a test that verifies this behavior. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01KpatzFdRne5Gb4cgggobdS","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01WmKACLwx1RXujVaNSZGfeS","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/BUG_ANALYSIS.md","content":"# Non-Legacy Mail Decryption Key Propagation Bug - Analysis Report\n\n## Summary\n\nA critical bug exists in the Tutanota codebase where **encrypted session keys are not propagated when loading supplementary mail data**. This causes non-legacy mails (mails using owner-encrypted session keys) to fail decryption, resulting in blank message bodies, missing reply-to addresses, and missing attachment listings.\n\n## Root Cause\n\n**Location**: `src/api/worker/search/MailIndexer.ts:733-785`\n\nThe bug is in the `loadMailDetails` method which loads related mail entities in bulk. When loading `MailDetailsBlob` or `MailDetailsDraft` entities, the method calls:\n\n```typescript\n// Line 733 - Buggy code\nconst mailDetailsBlobs = await this.loadInChunks(MailDetailsBlobTypeRef, listId, ids)\n```\n\nThe `loadInChunks` method (line 785) then calls:\n\n```typescript\n// Line 785 - Missing session keys!\nthis._entity.loadMultiple(typeRef, listId, chunk)  // No providedOwnerEncSessionKeys!\n```\n\n**The problem**: The `loadMultiple` call does NOT pass a `Map<Id, Uint8Array>` of `providedOwnerEncSessionKeys`.\n\n## How It Manifests\n\n1. Mail objects contain an `_ownerEncSessionKey` field that is encrypted with the mail owner group's key\n2. When loading child entities (MailDetailsBlob, MailDetailsDraft), this session key needs to be passed to `EntityRestClient.loadMultiple`\n3. Without this mapping, `EntityRestClient._handleLoadMultipleResult` cannot inject the `_ownerEncSessionKey` on the loaded entities\n4. The entities arrive at decryption with `sessionKey=null`\n5. Decryption fails silently, setting `_errors` on the entities\n6. Users see blank mail bodies, missing reply-to addresses, etc.\n\n## Correct Pattern (From MailUtils.loadMailDetails)\n\nThe correct implementation is already present in `src/mail/model/MailUtils.ts:404-411`:\n\n```typescript\n} else {\n  const mailDetailsId = neverNull(mail.mailDetails)\n\n  const providedOwnerEncSessionKeys = new Map<Id, Uint8Array>()\n  providedOwnerEncSessionKeys.set(elementIdPart(mailDetailsId), assertNotNull(mail._ownerEncSessionKey))\n  return entityClient\n    .loadMultiple(MailDetailsBlobTypeRef, listIdPart(mailDetailsId), [elementIdPart(mailDetailsId)], providedOwnerEncSessionKeys)\n    .then((d) => MailWrapper.details(mail, d[0].details))\n}\n```\n\n## How The Fix Works\n\n1. For each mail that references MailDetailsBlob/MailDetailsDraft, create a map entry:\n   - **Key**: The entity ID\n   - **Value**: The encrypted session key from the mail (`mail._ownerEncSessionKey`)\n\n2. Pass this map to `loadMultiple` as the fourth parameter\n\n3. `EntityRestClient._handleLoadMultipleResult` will then inject the session key:\n   ```typescript\n   // Line 276\n   instance._ownerEncSessionKey = providedOwnerEncSessionKeys.get(getElementId(instance))\n   ```\n\n4. Decryption succeeds because the session key is now available\n\n## Affected Code Paths\n\n### Bulk Loading (MailIndexer.loadMailDetails)\n\n- **Line 733**: Loading MailDetailsBlob entities\n  - Should pass Map<Id, Uint8Array> with mailDetailsBlobId -> mail._ownerEncSessionKey\n\n- **Line 749**: Loading MailDetailsDraft entities\n  - Should pass Map<Id, Uint8Array> with mailDetailsDraftId -> mail._ownerEncSessionKey\n\n### Single Entity Loading (Already Correct)\n\n- `src/mail/model/MailUtils.ts:410` - Correctly passes `providedOwnerEncSessionKeys`\n- `src/api/worker/search/MailIndexer.ts:154-162` - Correctly passes `mail._ownerEncSessionKey` to single `load` calls\n\n## Impact\n\nUsers affected by this bug experience:\n\n1. **Blank mail bodies** - The MailDetailsBlob content cannot be decrypted\n2. **Missing reply-to addresses** - The MailDetails.replyTos field cannot be decrypted\n3. **Missing attachment listings** - Cannot load attachment metadata\n4. **Silent failures** - Mail indexing fails silently with decryption errors\n5. **Search issues** - Mail indexer cannot index non-legacy mails properly\n\n## Test Coverage\n\nThe regression test in `/workspace/regression_test.test.ts` includes:\n\n1. **BUG_SCENARIO**: Demonstrates that decryption fails without session key\n2. **CORRECT_BEHAVIOR**: Shows decryption succeeds when session key is provided\n3. **FIX_PATTERN**: Demonstrates the proper injection pattern\n4. **BUG_REPRODUCTION**: Explicitly reproduces the MailIndexer bug\n5. **FIX_VERIFICATION**: Confirms the fix would solve the issue\n\n## Implementation Notes\n\nWhen implementing the fix:\n\n1. In `MailIndexer.loadMailDetails`:\n   - For MailDetailsBlob loading (line 733):\n     ```typescript\n     const providedOwnerEncSessionKeys = new Map<Id, Uint8Array>()\n     for (const mail of mailDetailsBlobMails) {\n       providedOwnerEncSessionKeys.set(elementIdPart(mail.mailDetails!), mail._ownerEncSessionKey!)\n     }\n     const mailDetailsBlobs = await this.loadInChunks(\n       MailDetailsBlobTypeRef,\n       listId,\n       ids,\n       providedOwnerEncSessionKeys  // Add this parameter\n     )\n     ```\n\n2. Update `loadInChunks` signature to accept and forward the session key map\n\n3. Both calls need to pass a `Map<Id, Uint8Array>` containing session keys indexed by entity ID.\n\n## Step-by-Step Fix\n\n### 1. This causes the session keys available in the parent Mail object to not be propagated to the loaded child entities, resulting in decryption failures.\n\n**Location:** `src/api/worker/search/MailIndexer.ts:733-785`\n\n## Test Coverage\n\n### Test 1: \"MailDetailsBlob decryption fails when session key is not provided (BUG SCENARIO)\"\n- **Purpose**: Demonstrates the
